Important News

Central Government and National Government's Memorial Week 64

The Central Party Headquarters held its 73rd weekly memorial service for Sun Yat-sen at 9:00 AM on the 18th in the Grand Hall. Central Committee members Sun Ke, Chen Guofu, Liu Lu, Chen Lifu, and other officials and guests, totaling approximately 500 to 600 people, attended. Chairman Sun Ke presided over the ceremony and reported that the Central Government's anti-rebel troops had achieved victories on the Tianjin-Pukou, Jiaoji (Jiaozhou-Jinan), and Longhai (Lanzhou-Haizhou) lines. The recapture of Jinan on the Tianjin-Pukou line on the 15th was particularly significant and sufficient to chill the rebels' courage and suppress the enemy's atmosphere. According to reports, Yan's rebel troops south of the Yellow River number no more than 60,000 to 70,000, and more than two-thirds of them have been disarmed and captured, with few remaining. The enemy on the Jiaoji line has been completely disarmed by the divisions of Han Fuju, Li Baobing, Liu Zhentang, and others, who launched attacks from multiple directions. Feng's rebel troops on the Longhai line made every effort to counterattack in an attempt to contain the Central Government's forces on the Tianjin-Pukou line. Upon learning that Jinan had been recaptured by our forces, they were terrified and reportedly retreated under cover from Lanfeng. The enemy troops can be completely resolved within the shortest possible time. For more than a decade, Yan Xishan has possessed troops for self-defense and has always used opportunistic methods to use others as sacrifices to consolidate his own territory. This time, his collusion with Feng was also to use Feng's strength to engage the Central Government's troops at the Longhai line, where the main force was located, and then concentrate his troops on the Tianjin-Pukou line to seize opportunities. Feng Yuxiang has plundered the wealth of the people of Shaanxi and Gansu in recent years to raise troops, and now his rear is unable to continue. This time, his collusion with Yan was also to use Yan's salaries and weapons to supply his needs. Therefore, the Central Government's recent strategy is to temporarily take a defensive stance on the Longhai line and actively advance on the Tianjin-Pukou line, using a large encirclement to annihilate Yan's rebel main force concentrated on the south bank of the Yellow River. Now the military and political situation in the north is fundamentally shaken, and the so-called expanded conference and the pseudo-government being prepared will collapse without being attacked and will not be able to survive. In the diplomatic arena, representatives of various countries in China, due to their lack of clear understanding of the Chinese situation and the Central Government's situation, have had to feign compliance with the reactionary elements in the north. For example, the Englishman Simpson, who was used by Yan's rebels to forcibly occupy the Tianjin Customs and help Chinese traitors, should also be punished under British law. The diplomatic authorities have repeatedly lodged protests, but there has been no response. Their psychology is nothing more than hoping that the warlords will win and enjoy special privileges in the north, expressing sympathy to the reactionary faction in an intangible way. Another example is the Japanese news agency, which has repeatedly fabricated rumors that are detrimental to the Central Government in the past and present military situation. Although facts have clarified that it is not worth laughing at, its consistent subjective intention to help Chinese rebels and hope that China's internal strife will be prolonged and never unified is obvious. The victory of the Central Government's troops this time may give the representatives of various countries in China a greater understanding of the Central Government, making them understand the principle of survival with support and death with opposition, and express sympathy. The economic aspect is also very related to the military situation. Since the rebellion occurred, the Shanghai public bond market has been shaken, and the tariff consolidation and demobilization bonds issued by the Central Government have fallen to 40% to 50%. Finance and banking have been severely affected. After the recapture of Jinan, they suddenly rose sharply again within a day or two and entered a stable trend. The final result of the military is to restore peace, consolidate unification, and implement political tutelage, and to thoroughly eliminate those who hinder peaceful unification, without perfunctoriness, without accommodation, and without accepting any conditions, so as not to repeat the mistakes of false peace and false unification. As for the Communist Party's arson, killing, and kidnapping in Hunan, Hubei, and Jiangxi provinces, it can give ignorant farmers and workers a deep understanding and prevent them from being deceived and driven forever. The Central Government's army will soon return and launch a thorough suppression, which can be completely eliminated. As for Wang Jingwei's character, he has a considerable history within the party. Since leaving the party and leaving the doctrine, his collusion with the Communist Party to plot reaction and sabotage the Central Government is undeniable. The Central Committee comrades were very fond of him, and did not impose severe punishment on him at the Third Plenary Session, hoping that he would repent behind closed doors and realize his mistakes. Unexpectedly, he ran out of road and joined the warlords and all reactionary factions to conspire rebellion. His insanity has reached this point, which can be said to be a lack of awareness until death. He did not bear any major responsibility in the party before and after the death of Sun Yat-sen, and his cooperation with Borodin to allow the Communist Party to manipulate power and undermine the Three Principles of the People is his sole responsibility. He was confused by his desire for leadership, and his one thought caused endless disasters, which is truly shameful and pitiful. The meeting adjourned after the report.

At 10:00 AM on the same morning, the National Government held a weekly memorial service for Sun Yat-sen. Gu Yingfen, Zhu Peide, Jiang Menglin, Liu Ruiheng, Zhang Nanxian, Niu Yongjian, Zhu Lühe, Lin Xiang, Chen Shaokuan, Zhou Yawei, Mu Xiangyue, Li Jinlun, Chen Yu, Wu Siyu, and other officials from the National Government's civil and military offices, totaling more than 200 people, attended. Chairman Gu Yingfen presided over the ceremony. Secretary Qian Changzhao gave a political report as follows: Jinan on the Tianjin-Pukou Railway has been captured, and the rebel troops have been almost completely eliminated. The Feng's rebel troops on the Longhai Railway have suffered several setbacks in their counterattacks, and our side has ample military strength. Now is the time to take advantage of the victory to pursue the attack. Our progress on the Peiping-Hankou Railway is also rapid, and it will not be difficult to capture Xuchang, Kaifeng, and Zhengzhou. In short, the end of the military affairs is not far away. After the end of this military affair, we will definitely get a long period of peace. Manpower and financial resources should be concentrated on construction projects, the vitality of society can be restored, and the crisis of the country's economic future can be reduced. Changsha has suffered great losses due to the Communist Party's disturbances. The State Council decided last Friday to allocate 100,000 yuan from the national treasury for urgent relief. As for the suppression of bandits in Hubei, Hunan, and Jiangxi provinces, Director He Yingqin is planning the overall plan. The three provinces have recently been rampant with the Communist Party, and the people have been displaced. The government has full responsibility for local security and should find ways to completely eliminate the problems once and for all. The State Council approved the London International Postal Convention last Friday. The International Postal Association held its ninth congress in London last year. The government briefly sent Shi Zhaoji, Minister to England, and Liu Shufan, Director of the Ministry of Communications, to participate. Later, because Minister Shi returned to China, only Representative Liu attended and signed one convention and six agreements. The ones signed by our representative were: the International Postal Convention, the International Postal Exchange Insurance Letter and Box Agreement, the International Postal Exchange Package Agreement, and the International Postal Money Order Agreement. This time, the government specifically approved them so that they could take effect as soon as possible.

Ministry of Railways to Issue Short-Term Bonds 65

To Purchase Vehicles for the Peiping-Liaoning Railway

The Ministry of Railways stated that the Peiping-Liaoning Railway Administration has repeatedly reported that the railway lacks locomotives, which affects transportation, and that the overall situation should be planned accurately to remedy the situation. It also stated that the railway's locomotives are originally insufficient. Among the various locomotives, 93 are between 29 and 41 years old, too old and too worn to be used for long. They should be stopped. Forcing them to be used not only reduces working hours due to repairs, but also delays transportation, allowing the South Manchuria Railway to absorb a large amount of goods. The tangible and intangible losses are enormous. Currently, the precarious maintenance relies on more than 40 locomotives from other railways that are temporarily retained for use to make up for the deficit. If they are returned, the power will be exhausted. Judging from the current freight situation, after the autumn harvest this year, the transportation of goods will inevitably increase several times compared to previous years. Currently, the transportation capacity is already lacking during the off-season, so the precarious situation at that time can be imagined. If a plan to purchase additional locomotives is not decided early, the opportunity will be missed, and both the railway and merchants will suffer. After ordering the relevant departments and sections to set up a locomotive purchase committee to conduct detailed research, the results of the research showed that in addition to retaining 44 locomotives from other railways, if the old vehicles can be repaired on schedule and no special circumstances occur on the line, a minimum of 12 passenger locomotives, 28 freight locomotives, and 2 shunting locomotives should be purchased, totaling 42 locomotives. After Gao Jiyi, Director of the Railway Bureau, invited the banking groups of Peiping and Tianjin to discuss cooperation repeatedly, he reached an agreement with Jincheng, Yanye, and Zhongnan Banks to deposit the funds for purchasing vehicles with the banks on a monthly basis, and planned to issue short-term bonds of 5 million yuan in two batches, which would be underwritten by the three banks. Currently, 20 locomotives are to be purchased first, and the regulations for the bonds have been drafted and submitted for review. Minister Sun reviewed the results and stated that the railway's lack of locomotives is indeed a fact, and there is competition from the South Manchuria Railway, so efforts should be made to catch up and remedy the situation. The estimated cost of the vehicles is approximately 3.6 million national currency. In addition to the Railway Bureau depositing the funds for purchasing vehicles on a monthly basis, bonds of 1.8 million yuan will still need to be issued. The remaining 3.2 million yuan in bonds will be sold after purchasing the second batch of locomotives. The method is appropriate. In addition to submitting the bond regulations to the Executive Yuan for forwarding to the Legislative Yuan for review and promulgation, it has been instructed that the Peiping-Liaoning Railway Administration must wait until the National Government promulgates the bond regulations before signing the vehicle purchase contract with the three banks.

The Southern Fujian Hubei Ocean Incident Has Been Resolved 66

Chen Guohui's Troops Have Complied with Orders to Withdraw

Xiamen Correspondence: Chen Guohui attacked the Hubei Ocean militia, and over eight hundred retreated to Xianyou. The Hubei Ocean refugees fled to the Xianyou, Nan'an, and Dehua regions, reaching twenty thousand. Yongchun County Chief Lin Zupei, Party Commissioner Liu Chengqing, militia representatives Liu Jimin and Guo Qixiang, appealed to military envoy Fang Shengtang and the provincial government. Overseas Chinese from Southern Fujian also sent telegrams to Fuzhou and Quanzhou, requesting action. The provincial government ordered Chen Guohui to withdraw the Hubei Ocean troops, and the First Regiment of the newly organized First Division, led by Wang Zuqing, took over defense to effectively prevent conflict. Lin Shouguo, brigade commander of the Second Marine Brigade in Xianyou, was also ordered to send troops to escort the refugees back to Hubei. After receiving the provincial order, Fang Shengtang personally went to Yongchun to meet with Chen Guohui and instructed him to comply with the order. Chen expressed his obedience. Fang returned to Quanzhou from Yongchun on the eighth, and on the ninth, he ordered Wang's regiment to depart from Quanzhou. On the eleventh, the advance troops of Chen Qifang's battalion arrived in Hubei. From that day on, Chen's troops began to withdraw, and by the thirteenth, Wang's entire regiment had arrived, and Chen's troops had completely withdrawn. After Wang's regiment departed, the Training Corps also continued to advance to Nan'an Honglai on the eleventh, connecting with Yong. On the eleventh, Fang sent He Xianzhu, former Fujian Salt Transport Envoy, to Hubei Ocean to investigate the people's disaster situation. On the twelfth, he reported back to Fang, who immediately telegraphed the provincial government, reporting the resolution of the Hubei Ocean Incident, roughly stating that Hubei Ocean was the gateway to Dehua and that troops were currently being concentrated from various routes. Chen's troops had to pass through Hubei Ocean on their way forward, and the Hubei Ocean militia had repeatedly seized military firearms, hence the conflict. The losses suffered by the people from burning and looting were also not as severe as rumored. After persuasion, Chen Guohui expressed his obedience and willingness to be the vanguard in the campaign against Lu, and he was preparing to advance on Dehua and Datian. The Hubei Ocean area had been ordered to have a company of troops from the Training Corps stationed there. Gao Jingli's (i.e., Gao Weiguo) troops had also been ordered to concentrate in Anhai, and the abandoned Huian defense area would also be taken over by a team from the Training Corps. According to news from the Yongchun Joint Association here, Chen Guohui's promise to withdraw the Hubei Ocean troops and serve as the vanguard against Lu is indeed a fact. However, because Hubei Ocean is close to Yongcheng and the militia's strength remains, there are fears of retaliation and a request for the reorganization of the Hubei Ocean militia and their transfer to the front. Fang Shengtang agreed that the Hubei Ocean militia would be reorganized by the Military Envoy's Office and would definitely not be allowed to cause trouble in the rear. However, whether they would be transferred to the front to fight against Lu was still undecided because the nature of the militia was a kind of self-defense organization for the people, and the government could not regard them as troops to be transferred at will. (August 15th)

Western Fujian Militia Recovers Longyan 67

Communist bandit Deng Yigang Flees to Longmen Creek

Fuzhou Correspondence: The main force in suppressing the communists in Western Fujian has recently shifted from the army to the militia. This militia can be divided into two parts: the Tingzhou area is the Tingzhou Armed Self-Defense Corps, led by Zhong Shaoying, with a total of more than 3,000 people, who have now defeated the communist bandits in Wuping and Shanghang and are advancing on Tingzhou. The Longyan area is the joint office of the five-county militia, led by Chen Zukang, also with more than 3,000 people, who have also wiped out the communist bandits in Hua'an and Zhangping counties and are now recovering Longyan. The plan is to attack in three routes: one route from Yanshi in Zhangping, one route from Yongfu in Hua'an, and one route from Shizhong in Yongding. After all three routes of the militia reach the border of Longyan, a general attack will be ordered on the communist bandits entrenched in Longyan. The bandit leader Deng Yigang has led more than a thousand people and fled to places such as Dachi and Longmen Creek. There are fewer than four or five hundred bandits in the city of Longyan. The Creek militia learned that Deng's bandits had retreated to gather in that area, and immediately gathered about a thousand people from the Yongfu militia to encircle them in different directions. After several days of fierce fighting, the communist bandits suffered heavy casualties. After the five-county militia attacked Longyan, the rear defense was also planned. The Yongfu area was temporarily handed over to the Hua'an militia, Zhan Fangqi, the Yanshi area to the Zhangping Security Team, Chen Guohua, and the Shizhong area to Sa Zhenbing. Sa has returned to Shizhong from Fushi.

Fujian's Finances After Government Downsizing 68

Still a Monthly Shortfall of 500,000 Yuan Starting in September

Fuzhou Correspondence: The Fujian Provincial Government implemented downsizing measures starting in August due to significant revenue shortfalls. It has now been found that each agency has laid off dozens of personnel, with some laying off as many as thirty or forty, and others laying off a dozen or twenty. The agencies being abolished are also close to completing their winding-up process, and it is expected that they will be completed within days. Although there are still one or two sections, such as the Provincial National Arts Hall and the Women's Factory, requesting to be retained, the provincial government has refused to allow them to be retained due to the overall relationship. However, there are also some that are closely related to the overall social life and cannot be cut, such as the West Lake Park, a recreational area for the people of Fuzhou. The monthly funding was originally set at 500 yuan, but this time it was completely cancelled, almost leading to its abandonment. Recently, after consultation between the park's director, Zheng Baja, and the Municipal Works Bureau, the bureau sent craftsmen to work, and Zheng volunteered to manage it, which barely maintained the status quo. In addition, the funding for the Consumer Cooperative, which specializes in the purchase and transport of rice and firewood to stabilize prices and regulate food supply, was originally set at 600 yuan per month, but has now been reduced to 200 yuan. The director of the cooperative, Wu Tong, has submitted a request to the provincial government to wind it up because he cannot maintain it. It is expected that after the cooperative is closed, firewood and rice merchants will inevitably take the opportunity to monopolize, which will hinder people's livelihoods. The laid-off employees of various agencies are currently organizing a petition group to request the provincial government to pay off their back wages so that those who are from this province can find other jobs, and those who are from other provinces can return to their hometowns as soon as possible.

However, downsizing is only one method of reducing expenditure. In terms of increasing revenue, He Gonggan, acting Director of the Finance Department and concurrently Finance Envoy, has drafted plans for reorganizing national and local taxes. However, because this province is still in the midst of the campaign against Lu and the suppression of communists, he has been unable to implement them. As a last resort, He borrowed 500,000 yuan from the Fuzhou General Chamber of Commerce using consumer taxes on tea and wood to cover military expenses. However, the various merchant guilds stated that since the outbreak of the war against Lu, river transport between the provincial capital and northern Fujian had been cut off, and commerce had been completely halted for two and a half months, making them unable to afford the loan. After convening two meetings by the Finance Department, they all requested the opening of river transport as a condition for the loan, so there has been no result. At the same time, the provincial government also received a telegram from the Ministry of Finance stating that the central government is currently implementing financial reorganization and will suspend the assistance of 150,000 yuan per month to Fujian province, and that the 130,000 yuan per month in salaries for Liu Heding's division should be borne by the local government of Fujian province starting in September, according to the recent State Council meeting's resolution that the salaries of the central government's troops stationed in various provinces should be borne by the local governments. The two items, calculated together, increase the shortfall by 280,000 yuan, which, added to the original shortfall of 200,000 yuan (Fujian province's monthly revenue and expenditure originally had a difference of 300,000 yuan, and this time the austerity measures reduced it by about 100,000 yuan), means that Fujian still has a monthly shortfall of 500,000 yuan after the government downsizing. Recently, Yang Shuzhuang is discussing solutions with He Gonggan and Chen Peikun, and has first sent Shi Jialin, Secretary-Director of the Finance Department, to Beijing to contact Minister Song of the Ministry of Finance for relief. As a last resort, during the military period, it is planned to temporarily extract customs duties, salt taxes, tobacco and alcohol taxes, and stamp taxes to meet urgent needs. (August 15th)

Chongqing Press Entirely Suspends Publication 69

To Resist Military Atrocities

The Chongqing press has been subjected to oppression by the military in recent years. In the recent past, for example, the Chongqing Express criticized a brigade commander Lan Wenbin of the Women's Association because his concubine, Ou, was a member of the Women's Association. He closed down the newspaper and arrested the chief writer, Shao Zhengchao, ordering him to bow three times to his concubine to apologize, otherwise he would be shot. Also, the Tuantuan News Agency revealed that the food and drink in the Shizhong Restaurant was unclean, which was a fact. However, the shareholder of the restaurant, Feng Shijun, who served as a quartermaster in Pan Wenhua's brigade, arbitrarily arrested the president and editor of the news agency and detained them for several days before releasing them. After these two incidents occurred, the Chongqing Press Association and the Reporters Association strongly protested to the authorities, but to no avail. Unexpectedly, on August 1, the local Xishu Evening News was suddenly destroyed by a bodyguard, and the equipment in the museum was smashed to pieces. The president, Li Chunyi, and several editors were seriously injured. When the bodyguards left, they said that the social news published by the newspaper in recent days had damaged the face of the generals in Chongqing, and ordered [T13]one[/T] that the smashing incident should not be reported to the authorities; [T13]two[/T] that the smashing situation should not be reported; [T13]three[/T] that an apology should be published in the newspaper to the generals. After this incident, the press unanimously aided the Xishu Evening News, issuing comments on one hand and presenting them to the 21st Army Headquarters, the City Defense Headquarters, and the Public Security Bureau on the other, requesting punishment of the murderers and guaranteeing the safety of the Xishu Evening News and other newspapers in Chongqing. However, the authorities remained unmoved, and on August 4, the Xishu Evening News was destroyed by bodyguards for the second time, and it was stated that the editors would be killed. For a time, everyone in the press was in danger, so the three organizations of the Press Association, the Reporters Association, and the News Agency Association unanimously decided to suspend publication entirely starting on the 5th to fight for the final victory, and issued a notice as follows: The local Xishu Evening News was suddenly destroyed by soldiers on the 1st of this month, and several days have passed without a proper resolution. Yesterday, the newspaper was destroyed again and the staff members were injured. The local associations believe that this matter is of great importance to the safety of the entire press and social security, and have convened an emergency joint meeting to unanimously decide to strike entirely from today onwards, and wait quietly for the public to decide. Work will resume after a proper resolution is obtained.

Soviet Russia Adds River Defense Gunboats 70

Patrolling the Heilongjiang and Wusuli Rivers, a Total of Thirty Ships Monopolize the Heilongjiang and Wusuli Shipping Routes, Detaining Our Sailing Ships

Harbin Correspondence: After the river opened this year, the large Soviet Russian warships patrolled the Heilongjiang and Wusuli rivers once at the beginning of the river thaw, but due to the Vladivostok riots, they all sailed to the southwest areas such as Waizi to set up defenses. All the defenses of the Heilongjiang and Wusuli rivers were replaced by thirty shallow-water steamships built by the Bolly Military Factory. Each ship was equipped with two small steel cannons and two machine guns, and carried thirty sailors managed by one naval lieutenant junior grade. It can travel 80 li per hour. Since May, they have been successively launched into the water and patrolled in sections. Whenever Chinese ships travel to the mainstream of the Wusuli and Heilongjiang rivers, these steamships will chase after them, sometimes firing shots to prevent them from sailing. When the Chinese ships stop, the boats quickly sail away. Such incidents have occurred repeatedly, and our commercial ships have no way to avoid them. On July 10, a Chinese man named Sun Shitou and several crew members were driving a sailing ship loaded with thirty live pigs from Tongjiang to Hulin. At noon on July 12, when they arrived near Tuantuanzi, the border between Suiyuan, the sailing ship lost control due to strong winds and was blown to the Russian shore. The 11th Russian border guard saw them and rushed out dozens of soldiers from the shore to intercept the ship. The ship was unable to move forward and obeyed the order to approach the Russian shore. After the ship docked, the Russian soldiers boarded the boat and took Sun Shitou and others away to the barracks. The Russian officials interrogated them and said that the boat should not have approached the Russian shore. They asked whether they wanted to be dealt with officially or privately. Sun asked what the difference was between being dealt with officially or privately. The Russian official said that if they were dealt with officially, the ship, cargo, and people would be sent to a prison in Bolly and detained for two years before being released. If they were dealt with privately, the people would be released and the ship and cargo confiscated. Sun knew the darkness of the Russian prison in Bolly, so he was willing to let the people go and let them dispose of the ship and cargo. That night, the Russians used a ship to send Sun and others back to our shore. Sun and others then reported to the Suiyuan County Government, but the county's negotiations were ineffective. Since this incident, Chinese ships sailing on the Wusuli and Heilongjiang rivers have been wary. However, this year, Hulin, Raohe, and Suiyuan are rich in opium, and about 100,000 people have gone there to work in the labor sector for several months. Therefore, the shifts of ferrying passengers and goods are profitable, and they still compete to go there despite the difficulties. Currently, there are six Chinese ships sailing on the Wusuli River and four on the Heilongjiang River. (13th)

Russian Spies Captured in Manzhouli 71

Russian Bu Chengyanzi is a Russian Spy

Harbin Correspondence: The Manzhouli garrison suspected that someone was secretly communicating with the Russian border guards because our recent military movements and border situation were being detected by the Russian side in great detail. About half a month ago, they made every effort to find out and learned that a Russian worker (Maoluo Zuofu) at an iron factory was a Russian military secret agent, and they found a secret code communication. The military police arrested him and sent him to Habu. However, the Russian consuls in Manzhouli and Habu successively protested, saying that Maoluo Zuofu was a legitimate worker. The authorities did not release him because the case involved military espionage. Unexpectedly, on the 11th of this month, the special police in Manzhouli arrested another Russian spy named Bu Chengyanzi, who was a businessman in Manzhouli who usually claimed to be a White Party member but was actually a complete Red Russian. It is said that last year's capture of Manzhouli and the fall of Zhalannuoer were due to this person privately drawing maps in advance and giving them to the Russian army, so they were familiar with the roads as if they were in an uninhabited area. Otherwise, our army would not have collapsed so quickly. After the Russian army entered Manzhouli last year, Bu Chengyanzi served as the interim mayor, managing everything in the city and searching for our hidden officers. This year, after the Russian army withdrew, Bu Chengyanzi still lived among the White Party, privately probing our military situation and reporting it to the Russian army. The Manzhouli military police have found factual evidence and arrested him. He was escorted to Harbin yesterday and interrogated once by the Special Police Management Office. His confession was cunning and he has not admitted it yet. However, the Manzhouli authorities said that after this person was arrested, Manzhouli can have a few less troubles. (11th)

The following important cases were resolved: [T13]one[/T] Request the County Education Bureau to add a social education guidance specialist. [T13]three[/T] Submit a request to the Education Department and the County Government to transfer Wuxi Park to the management of the Education Bureau in order to comply with the regulations. [T13]four[/T] Send a letter to the Education Bureau instructing all public and private schools in the county to pay attention to promoting their careers. [T13]five[/T] This association should organize a people's drama troupe. [T13]six[/T] Send a letter to the People's Education Center requesting the addition of public equipment for the use of the public to facilitate circulation. [T13]seven[/T] Request the Education Bureau to allocate funds to this association annually. [T13]eight[/T] Request the Education Bureau to reward and subsidize private people who request public education services. [T13]nine[/T] Send a letter to the Shanghai Student Association requesting that Pingjiao be changed to Minjiao, and request the County Education Bureau to instruct the association not to hold fund-raising activities without authorization. [T13]ten[/T] Election of executive committee members: Qin Liufang, Miao Shaoping, Rui Ziyu, Shen Xianzhi, Xu Xiyan, Hua Jinji, Yin Zhaohua, Qian Zuomin, Song Yongsun, and other nine people were elected as executive committee members.

Storing Dry Cocoons Causes Disputes. Xin Jichen, a shareholder of the Ganxin Silk Factory under the Workers' Bridge in this county, stored the spring cocoons he collected in a pile near the factory last year during the spring cocoon泛中. Later, the cocoon merchants sold them separately. It was estimated that more than ten piculs were missing. Later, Xin seriously negotiated with the pile, and the pile paid out considerable losses. Yuan Fuchen, an executive committee member of the Cocoon Industry Association, also stored the spring cocoons he collected in the pile last year. When the cocoons were reeled, five or six piculs were missing. In addition, Yang Ruizhang, Gao Jigeng, Hua Agen, and other porters purchased 402 bags of dry cocoons in Chuanmen Bridge and stored them in Fuyu Stack, and about eight piculs were missing. Yang Ruizhang and others have now lodged serious representations with the stack, and it is not known how it will be resolved.

Changzhou 78

A Fishing Boat in Xinzhazhen Was Robbed. A fishing boat was moored near the Daqiao River in Xinzhazhen, Wuyi County. The other morning, ten bandits suddenly boarded the boat, each holding a sharp blade, and robbed the boat. The boat owner, Sun Jigen, was grabbed and stabbed six or seven times. Sun was seventy-five years old and suffered a serious head injury. He was then taken to Wujin Hospital for treatment.

A Shop Assistant Was Wounded by a Stray Bullet. Zhang Chuansheng, a shop assistant at the Jiufu Store on Xizhi Street, Wuyi County, is from Guotangqiao in the northern township. On the afternoon of the 16th, Zhang was going home when he passed through Zhoujinbu Village in Dabatou. A police team was surrounding and arresting bandits in the village, and gunshots rang out constantly. Zhang was unable to escape and was shot in the back. The bullet exited from his right shoulder, and the blood flowed like a stream. He was seriously injured and collapsed to the ground. His family carried him to the hospital for treatment that night. He has not yet been out of danger.

Zhenjiang 79

The Zhenjiang Office Orders the Opening of a Joint Defense Conference. The Jiangsu Provincial Security Office stated that since the bandit communists in the counties of Jiangbei, Tongru, Haimen, and Taixian had been severely suppressed by the provincial and county police teams, most of them had dispersed and the local area had been slightly stabilized. However, the remaining bandits were lurking and could not guarantee that they would not cause trouble again. Yesterday, the Security Office issued a telegram to Li Changjiang, commander of the Third Security Regiment, ordering him to order all counties under his jurisdiction to convene a bandit suppression joint defense conference in Tong on August 20 to discuss fundamental eradication measures and to submit the conference situation to the Office and the Civil Affairs Department for review and decision.

A Bad Monk at Guanyin Temple Was Arrested. The bad monk Jiao Yan at Guanyin Mountain in Nanmen destroyed forests, raped women, gathered people to gamble, and often used heretical remarks to confuse the public. The forest farm telegraphed the Zhenjiang County Chief to arrest him. The county has ordered the police to detain him for interrogation.

Nantong 80

The Ministry Orders the County Government to Recover the Military Office. The Ministry of Military Administration of the Military Government sent a commission to Tong to investigate and find that the old Langshan General's Office was occupied by Ma Haisan. On the 17th, it ordered the county government to recover it within a few days and take temporary custody of it for disposal.

Building Refreshed Towers to Defend Against Bandits in Tong Township. The local bandits in various districts of the eastern township of Tong have recently colluded with pirates to cause great trouble. After discussion by the party, government, military, and police, it was decided to build blockhouses in key areas along the southeastern coast to guard them. Yu Donger and other places have built them. On the 18th, various sectors were invited to inspect the artillery.

Jiangyin 81

Further Inquiry into the Case of the Water Police Captain Transporting Opium: The Fortress Headquarters seized a patrol boat of the 20th Detachment of the Water Police Corps, captained by Chen Bingquan, for transporting opium on behalf of opium traffickers in Liuwei Port the night before last. Nine individuals, including the boat occupants and opium traffickers, were apprehended. During the military trial on the 16th, they all confessed, and Chen Bingquan stated that he was ordered by the detachment commander, He Zhanao, to receive the opium. Due to the severity of the case, involving a public official, namely the commander of the water police, in opium trafficking, Commander Yang and County Magistrate Li have telegraphed their superiors for instructions. It is also reported that Commander He went to the district headquarters in Guazhou yesterday to personally explain everything.

The Kidnapping and Robbery Case in Shenli Townships: Liu Zifan and Liu Zijun, farmers in Liutieli, Shengang, were wealthy households in the area. Liu Zifan has passed away, leaving behind two sons: the elder, Jiaxiang, aged 13, and the younger, Yunxiang, aged 9. On the evening of the 16th at 8 PM, over twenty bandits kidnapped the elder son, Jiaxiang. His mother begged for the younger son's release. Before leaving, the bandits demanded a ransom of 2,000 yuan. His uncle and mother have no means to pay. Also, on the 16th, the Qian Gengchan family in Lugou Village, Licheng, was attacked by several bandits. Gengchan and his wife, Ms. Ding, were tied up, and an attempt to extort money failed. Ms. Ding was shot and killed, and an ox was taken away. The 6th Sub-bureau of the Public Security Bureau, fearing the bandits' strength, did not dare to pursue after hearing the alarm.

Gaoyou 82

Salary Demanding Meeting of Urban and Rural Teachers: The urban and rural teachers of this county are panicking because Acting Bureau Chief Sun Weixian has been in office for a long time but has only paid one month's salary. The remaining three months' salary is still outstanding. Therefore, they gathered at the library at 3 PM yesterday (the 15th) to discuss ways to demand their salaries. They decided to send the principals of various schools to the Education Bureau to demand their salaries. If this is unsuccessful, all urban and rural teachers will go to the Education Bureau to sit in protest.

Details of the Robbery in Shagou Town: Shagou Town originally had the 5th Squad of the 2nd Company of the County Police, stationed under Squad Leader Zhang. Later, Squad Leader Zhang was transferred to become the 8th Squad Leader under the order of Company Commander Li of the county seat. Shi Fulong was appointed to fill the vacant position. On the morning of the 4th of this month at 11 AM, just as the old and new squad leaders were taking over, all the soldiers of the 5th Squad mutinied. They shot and killed the new Squad Leader Shi Fulong, Special Agent Yao, and a servant. They also seized seven firearms from the 10th Squad stationed in the area and killed a soldier surnamed Yuan. Subsequently, they robbed several shops. After the robbery, the mutineers fled northeast. Before an hour had passed, the mutineers colluded with over two hundred bandits and returned to Shagou, looting the entire town. The total loss of all shops and households is estimated to be over 100,000 yuan. Local organizations have established a post-disaster committee and have reported the case to the provincial and county governments, requesting them to send personnel to investigate and dispatch troops to pursue and suppress the bandits.

Jiaxing 83

Scheduled Acceptance of Public Funds and Properties in Various Districts: The public funds and properties of various districts in Jiaxing are to be transferred to the district public offices for management. The county government has also issued an order to complete the transfer by August 31st. Upon receiving the order, the district chiefs have contacted the custodians of public funds and properties in their respective districts to arrange the handover dates in order to complete the transfer on schedule. It is reported that Zhao Taiqi, the custodian of public funds and properties in the 1st District, has agreed with District Chief Mei Shouren to hand over on August 30th and is currently preparing for the transfer. As for the township districts, because the autonomous regions have been changed to seven districts while the custodians of public funds and properties remain in eight districts, the custodians will create a detailed inventory and hand over the items by district at the designated time to clarify responsibilities and authority.

Huzhou 84

Kidnapping of Shi Guangyuan's Grandson: Shi Guangyuan, a farmer in Taiziwan, about ten li northwest of the city, is over sixty years old and has some wealth. His son died early, leaving behind a widowed daughter-in-law, Ms. Meng, and a grandson who is only five years old. Guangyuan was kidnapped by bandits in the winter of the 17th year and was ransomed for a large sum. However, the elderly and frail Guangyuan suffered from a nervous disorder after this ordeal. Moreover, due to poor cocoon yields and a bad autumn harvest in recent years, his family's situation is not as good as it used to be. Fortunately, the widowed daughter-in-law, Ms. Meng, has managed the household well and is still able to make ends meet. Unexpectedly, at around 6 PM on the 15th, more than ten bandits armed with guns suddenly arrived. Ms. Meng was cooling off at home, holding her five-year-old grandson in her arms and had no time to escape, resulting in her son being kidnapped by the bandits. They left a letter demanding a ransom of 4,800 yuan. The local defense corps was informed of the incident and immediately organized guards to pursue, but the bandits were nowhere to be found. It is reported that Ms. Meng does not have such a large sum of money to pay the ransom and is grieving all day long.

Xiaoshan 85

Villagers Destroy Township Office: The Dayi Township Office in the 5th District of Xiaoshan was ordered to prepare for the collection of self-government household donations. However, villagers from Kongjia and other villages resisted the donations, gathered crowds to beat the preparation staff member Wang Meiyu, and on the 12th, gathered over a hundred people to the township office to forcibly demand food and drink and destroy many pots, bowls, and other utensils. They threatened to beat up the preparation staff members. The township office, witnessing this situation, has reported the matter to the provincial and county governments, requesting severe punishment to deter lawlessness.

Shangyu 86

Robbery in Shangpu Town: At around 7 PM last night, over ten bandits speaking with a Sheng accent suddenly appeared on the streets of Shangpu Town in the western countryside. The bandits held guns and guarded the key locations on the street and threw over ten sulfur bombs to show their power. The remaining bandits first broke into the Lao Hengtai Rice Shop on the main street. They pulled out handguns and intimidated the shop owner, Wang Linfengxiang, into silence. They searched and robbed the store of over 400 yuan in cash that had been accumulated from daily business. Then, they went to the Wu Changmao Grocery Store on the middle street. The owner, Wu Ayun, was unable to escape and was captured. They forced him to hand over valuables, resulting in the loss of over 100 yuan and dozens of items of clothing. The bandits were not satisfied and planned to rob the Ren Dechang Butcher Shop. However, upon hearing the townspeople beat gongs, they opened fire and fled. Afterwards, Xu Jiayun, the special agent of the Haozhen Security Team, led the team to pursue, but the bandits had already disappeared without a trace.

Letters to the Editor

Letter from Yang Baoshen 87

To the Editor:

Your newspaper's Changshu correspondence on the 17th of this month reported that Branch Chief Tang Baoshen had absconded. This is completely untrue. Baoshen requested leave on the 11th of the month for official business to go to the province. The claim that only 40 taels of the 500 taels of Sichuan opium seized were handed over to the headquarters is also a complete lie. The News Daily reported on the 14th of this month that only 40 taels of 300 taels of opium seized were handed over. This shows that the reporters who submitted the news to both newspapers obtained inaccurate information. Moreover, several police officers were involved in the seizure of the opium this time. Not only do local people know the whole story of the case, but also all agencies and organizations. It is clear that Baoshen could not have embezzled the opium. I am deeply concerned that this will cause confusion. Therefore, I am writing to request a correction and hope that you will publish it.

Tang Baoshen, Chief of the 13th Public Security Branch of Changshu

Educational News

The Physical Education Chinese Expedition Football Team Wins Two Matches in Surabaya 88

Wins over Surabaya Selection Team by Three to Two; Another Win over the Ethiopian Team by Two to One; Eighth and Ninth Match Results of the Expedition Team

Situation of Victory over Surabaya Selection Team 89

(Surabaya Correspondence, August 2nd) After the Chinese Expedition Football Team was defeated by the weak Central Java Chinese Selection Team, the Surabaya Chinese Football Association was deeply concerned that it would greatly affect the welcome and the presale of tickets was unusually slow. Only about 3,000 shields were collected the night before the match. Who knew that the admiration of people from various ports for the skills of the Chinese Expedition Team athletes would not decrease because of this? Therefore, on the day of the match, Saturday (August 2nd), people from various ports around Surabaya flocked to watch. The streets were filled with cars and horses. By 12 o'clock, the entrance tickets at all distribution points had been sold out. At 2 o'clock, the spectators, in order to grab a position, braved the heat and flocked to the venue. Those who had not purchased entrance tickets also rushed to the venue. By 4 o'clock, the surroundings of the venue were already overcrowded. Even the roofs of nearby houses were filled with spectators. It is reported that the revenue on that day was about 15,000 shields.

(1) Applause as the Athletes Enter the Venue 90

At 4:30, the Chinese team athletes arrived in a long-distance car and entered the venue by bypassing the Nianshi Airport. After changing clothes in the changing room, they walked in through the main entrance with the Surabaya Selection Team in an orderly manner. The entire venue burst into thunderous applause. After the two teams were photographed, they chose their positions. The Chinese team was on the east and the Surabaya team occupied the west. The Chinese team's lineup was as follows:

Zhou Xianyan, Li Ning, Feng Yunyou, Chen Zhenhe, Chen Guangyao, Li Huitang, Sun Sijing, Dai Linjing, Chen Yutian, An Yuansheng, Cao Guisheng

(2) All-Out Effort in the Fierce Battle 91

After the two sides arranged their lineups, the referee issued the order to start the match. The president of the Surabaya Football Association entered the venue to perform the opening kickoff ceremony. The center forward received the ball and attacked with the left and right wings. Li Qiuguai and Chen Yutian passed the ball to each other, and their connection was excellent. The left and right wings also followed and advanced. However, they were stopped by the center back, Xilong, at the opponent's defensive line. The Surabaya front line counterattacked, and An Yuansheng closely monitored Wahis and was unable to do anything. Although he occasionally got the ball, he could only pass it to the left and right wings and was stopped by Xiao Heitan. Li Ning's tackling skills were excellent and he did not let go at all. Sun Sijing, sitting in the center, fought bravely despite his injury. The enemy found it difficult to succeed. Zhou's iron gate was as solid as a wall, repeatedly rescuing and defending, and the enemy could do nothing. Feng Yunyou dealt with the ball with his head and feet and did not loosen his step. The five forwards were full of revenge and fought with twice the strength as before, charging into the enemy's formation and making it impossible for them to defend. The left and right wingers attacked together, and the enemy was in a critical situation. Li Huitang played despite his illness. Although it was difficult for him to run and his shots were weak, his passing skills were superb and wonderful, which was admirable. Center forward Dai was unstoppable when breaking through the formation. He did not show any fatigue after seventy minutes. Right winger Chen's passing skills were excellent. Since he had not been on the field for a long time, he lacked energy. The left and right wingers were accurate in breaking through the formation and passing the ball. These two players were the most effective in winning the victory.

(3) Chen Yutian's Undeniable Contribution 92

Five minutes after the start of the match (4:48), Chen Yutian received the ball and broke through the formation, going straight into the enemy's heart after passing two defensive lines. Seeing that the situation was hopeless, Jiu Xing, who was chasing from behind, could only make a lucky bet to save the situation. He pushed Yutian down from behind. The referee noticed this and awarded a twelve-step penalty kick. Dai Linjing stepped forward to take the penalty. The whistle blew, and Center Forward Dai kicked the ball diagonally into the corner of the net. The whole audience burst into thunderous applause. The success of this goal was due to Chen Yutian's single-handed risk control, and his contribution was truly undeniable. Then, in the subsequent battle, the Chinese team had the upper hand and its military power was greatly enhanced. The spirit of the members of the front and rear coordinated attack teams was redoubled.

(4) Li Qiuguai Scores Despite the Pain 93

Three minutes after the resumption (4:51), General Cao broke through the enemy's defenses along the sideline and went straight up to a suitable point. He crossed the ball, and Li Qiuguai chased it. Seeing that the opportunity could not be missed, he kicked the ball straight into the goal despite the pain. The point of impact was excellent, and the goalkeeper was unable to defend it. Applause rose again. After the restart, the Chinese team still had a stronger position. The Surabaya Selection Team was still under attack, and the front line repeatedly returned to defend and was able to turn danger into safety. During the intense battle, the referee made many mistakes due to poor eyesight. At 5:06, the enemy's center back saw the ball coming and was unable to defend it, so he hit it with his hand. Outcries arose, but the referee did not notice it. Then, the offender did the same thing again and again, but the referee did not notice it. At 5:06, when the battle was urgent, Zhou's iron gate received a dangerous ball. The enemy was attacking, and the iron gate stopped to defend it. The referee, seeing it unclear from a distance, suspected that he had stepped over the line, so he blew the whistle and awarded a free kick. Fortunately, the defense was tight and the ball was rejected.

(5) Enemy Takes Advantage of the Weak Defense 94

At 5:11, the left wing Xiao Heitan went out but did not return, and the defensive line was weak. The enemy's right wing received the ball and ran straight up, folding into the center and approaching the goal. He shot fiercely at the goal. Zhou's iron gate dived to defend it, but it was too late, and the ball went into the net. After fighting for a few more minutes, the referee blew the whistle to rest.

(6) Exciting Continuation of the Battle 95

In the second half, the two sides changed battlefields, and the battle became more intense. Each side tried its best, and the excitement was very spectacular. The ball had no fixed direction, and the strength of the two sides was equal. The Chinese side had just cleared the ball when the Surabaya side was in danger again. The athletes on both sides flew like swallows, and were wonderful everywhere. After more than ten minutes of fierce battle, the two sides had not scored again.

(7) Center Forward Cai Makes a Timely Move 96

At 5:37, Xiao Heitan snatched the enemy's ball and dribbled it up. Seeing that the enemy was blocking him, he passed it lightly to Qiuguai. Qiuguai received the ball and took advantage of the situation to pass the ball over the enemy's defender's head. Center Forward Dai, knowing the opportunity, ran quickly to catch up and went straight into the enemy's heart. The goalkeeper was unable to defend it, so it was shot into the net for the third goal. After being defeated by three goals, the Surabaya Selection Team tried its best to counterattack in order to fight with its back to the wall. The left and right wings advanced together, and the momentum was fierce. However, the Chinese Expedition Team's defense was solid and could not be broken.

(8) China Ultimately Wins by Three to Two 97

At 4:46, the enemy's charge was too fierce, and the left wing Wahis was injured and fell to the ground. Seeing this, An Yuansheng's heart was moved with compassion. Not taking victory or defeat as the premise, but with humanity as the focus, he no longer chased the ball and quickly caressed Wahis. Zhou's iron gate also saw this and no longer paid attention to the football, but paid attention to Wahis's situation. Seeing that the referee still did not blow the whistle, the Surabaya forward shot the ball straight towards the Chinese team's goal. Zhou's iron gate could not defend it, and it was sent into the net. The Westerners cheered and applauded, while the Chinese remained silent. Since then, the Surabaya team tried its best to counterattack in order to seek revenge. The Chinese team did not give way at all and ultimately failed to score. After ten minutes of fierce battle, the two sides did not score again. As a result, the Chinese Expedition Team won by a score of three to two. After the referee blew the whistle to end the match, the audience cheered and dispersed. The Chinese team re-entered the venue to receive the commemorative cup and then led the team back to their residence. The sound of congratulations echoed from east to west until they reached the hostel.

(9) Victory and Defeat Do Not Make a Hero 98

After recording the battle situation, the reporter will say a few words to the readers. The Chinese Expedition Football Team's trip to Europe and then to Java was not smooth, and the talents were insufficient, and there was no reinforcement. Therefore, in each battle, the soldiers were mostly injured and played despite illness. We should forgive them for their defeat, and we should praise them even more for their victory. Victory and defeat are common in military affairs. We cannot hate them for their defeat or reward them for their victory. This attitude is not adopted by the wise. The true meaning of sports is not to take victory or defeat as honor or disgrace. There must be victory or defeat in the confrontation between the two armies. If the performance is excellent, even if they unfortunately lose, there is no disgrace in defeat. If the skills are equal, and they win only because of better luck, there is no glory in winning. Therefore, although the performance of the Chinese Football Expedition Team in the games held in various ports is not as good as last year, they have also won and lost, and amazing skills are often displayed. Therefore, we should respect the art of the athletes of the team as always, and never scold them for their failure, so as not to lose our own personality. If victory and defeat are common in military affairs, the Chinese Expedition Team's defeat to the Central Java Chinese Selection Team and victory over the Surabaya Selection Team is even more convincing.

(10) Wipe Out the Old Shame and Make People Happy 99

The so-called Surabaya Selection Team is the champion of this year's various port selection teams, and its strength is well known. Last year, Yuehua's Southern Expedition was only defeated by the Surabaya Selection Team in eleven games. Therefore, this time, in the minds of the compatriots, the victory or defeat of the games in various ports has become an unquestioned imagination. If they can defeat the Surabaya Selection Team to wipe out last year's shame, then their wishes will be fulfilled. Now that the goal has been achieved and the wishes have been fulfilled, the team's revenge to wipe out the shame is truly gratifying.

Victory over the Ethiopian Team 100

(Surabaya Correspondence, August 3rd) After the Chinese Expedition Football Team defeated the Surabaya Selection Team on Saturday, their reputation soared. Therefore, the second match with the Ethiopian team on Sunday (August 3rd) was even more attention-grabbing. Although the number of spectators was not as crowded as the first day, there were still quite a few. At 4:30, the Chinese team arrived with great prestige. Although they had been fighting fiercely for several days, they did not show any fatigue. After the photo was taken, the referee blew the whistle to assemble the team and choose the field. The Chinese team was on the west and the Ethiopian team occupied the east. The Chinese team's lineup was as follows:

Zhou Xianyan, Li Ning, Feng Lianyou, Chen Zhenhe, Sun Sijing, An Yuansheng, Chen Guangyao, Li Huitang, Dai Linjing, Chen Yutian, Cao Guisheng

(1) Order to Start, the Two Armies Open Fire 101

At 4:40, after the two sides arranged their lineups, the referee ordered to start the match. The Ethiopian team's front line dribbled the ball and attacked, but only reached the defensive line and returned. After the Chinese team's front line received support from the back line, they counterattacked like a tide, trying their best to resist. The Ethiopian team's back line was not weak either, trying their best to resist. The intense battle was very spectacular. The Ethiopian team's front line tried to attack, but the Chinese team defended step by step and ultimately failed to succeed. At this time, neither side was willing to give in, and the fierce attack and strong defense were evenly matched. In twenty minutes, both sides had not scored.

(2) Chen Guangyao Opens the Scoring 102

At exactly 5:00, Chen Yutian received support from the back line and dribbled the ball straight up. Seeing an opportunity, Chen Guanghui ran quickly into the interior. Seeing that the back line was empty, Yutian passed the ball to Guanghui, who chased up and raised his right foot to shoot fiercely. The ball went into the net, and the whole audience applauded and cheered. Then, in the subsequent battle, the Ethiopian team's front line tried its best to attack in order to retaliate, sending long passes and long shots step by step.

(3) Tie Due to Penalty Kick 103

When the ball was only two points away from entering the net, the enemy's counterattack was due to An Yuansheng's failure to defend, far away from the defensive zone. The left wing passed the ball in the middle, and Zhou's iron gate came out to rescue, but failed to get the ball, which came towards the goal. Xiao Heitan ran forward to rescue. It was expected that when the ball landed, it accidentally touched Xiao Heitan's hand. The referee noticed this and blew the whistle, awarding a twelve-point free kick. Although Zhou's iron gate tried hard to defend, he was ultimately scored on due to being approached. Therefore, a tie was created. Afterwards, in order to win, both sides tried their best to defend and attack. The intense battle was colorful, and the defensive lines of the two sides were repeatedly in danger. Dangerous balls frequently appeared at the goal, but fortunately, both sides were lucky, and both sides did not score. After fifteen minutes of intense battle, the referee blew the whistle to rest. The first half ended in a one-to-one tie.

(4) Two Great Generals Miss the Goal 104

In the second half, after the Chinese team moved the ball, they launched a large-scale attack. Chen Yutian received the ball and quickly passed it to the right wing, and the Flying General chased up like lightning and broke through the enemy's formation. The Ethiopian team's back line was helpless to stop him. The Flying General went straight to the heart and passed the ball horizontally to the center. Center Forward Dai, Chen Guanghui rushed up, but because he had not increased his speed, he missed the opportunity. After the Dragon side's goalkeeper passed the ball out, the Ethiopian team's front line launched a fierce attack like a tide, but Xiao Heitan was flying all over the field, blocking with his head and feet. In addition, the Chinese team's defense was assisting in all directions, and the enemy's plan was not successful.

(5) Chen Yutian Succeeds in the End 105

The Chinese team then came back strongly, and the back line went forward to provide support, and the left and right sides attacked together, and the enemy's goal was in danger. Although Li Qiuguai played despite his illness, he was still wonderful and had many wonderful passes and dribbling skills, and there was constant praise. At 5:25, the ball was hovering in the enemy's goal area, with feet passing and heads sending. One hook from Li Qiuguai and one header from Center Forward Dai, and the ball fell at Chen Yutian's feet. Yutian did not disappoint everyone and raised his foot to shoot fiercely. The goalkeeper was unable to defend, and the ball went into the net. Continuing the battle, the Ethiopian team wanted to fight with their backs to the wall and mobilized the entire team to attack, but the Chinese team's defense was stable and was rejected. The Chinese team's front line then led the team to counterattack, and the Flying General on the right wing showed his skills to the fullest, winning continuous applause. He charged and broke through the enemy, with incredible success.

(6) Li Qiuguai's Sick Foot Is Not Working 106

At 5:40, the Flying General broke straight into the formation and encountered an enemy. He passed it in the middle, and Chen Yutian passed it smoothly to Qiuguai. Although Qiuguai saw that the enemy's defensive line was empty, he knew that football could not support him and was afraid that reinforcements would chase him, so he took advantage of the situation to shoot fiercely at the goal. Unexpectedly, his sick foot was not working, and he actually exceeded the height, and the audience could not help but sigh. Later, after another ten minutes of fighting, although the battle was intense, the two sides did not score. When the referee blew the whistle to end the game, the score was two to one, and the Chinese team won again. The crowd went home happily. The Chinese team members went to the changing room to drink lemon to quench their thirst, and then formed a team to the field to receive the award before leaving the field and taking a car back to their residence.

Athletics Competition Held in Berlin and Tokyo 107

Berlin Wins

Scoring 65.5 Points; Japan 48.5 Points

(Berlin Telegraph, August 17th) Today, Berlin and Tokyo held an athletics competition. As a result, Berlin won with 65.5 points in 11 events, and Japan lost with 48.5 points.

Reason for the Loss: There is no doubt that the strength of the German army is superior, but the withdrawal of two Osaka players in the last minute inevitably shook the morale of the army and the situation was treacherous. According to the competition's nature, the reason for their withdrawal is that it is a competition between the two capitals, not an international one.

Each Has Advantages: Japan's Sumiyoshi in the javelin, Oda in the long jump, and Nishida in the pole vault all ranked first. Kimura's long jump was tied with Germany. Germany's advantages were mostly in track events, such as short and long distance running, high and low hurdles, and relay running.

Crowds Gather: The two armies held a competition at the Caroton Sports Ground, with more than 10,000 spectators, which was extremely grand. The inside of the venue was full of Japanese emblems, and there was a music team playing the national anthems of the two countries. On that day, it rained heavily, and it was deeply feared that the event would not be able to proceed as usual. As the athletes of the two armies entered the venue, the sunlight shot out from the clouds. Guests at the venue included Japanese Prince Takamatsu and his wife, and from Germany, former Tokyo Ambassador Dr. Schaff and current Tokyo Ambassador Dr. Frauches. The two armies worked very hard, but there were no special new records due to the muddy ground and strong winds.

Rotary Cup Preliminary Round Completed 108

Yesterday, the United States Fiercely Defeated Japan

No Games Today; Semifinals on the 21st: United States vs. Great Britain; China vs. Portugal

Yesterday was the third day of the Rotary Cup International Tennis Tournament preliminary round. It started at 4:30 PM at the Chinese Tennis Ground. There were two singles and two doubles groups. The order of the United States vs. Japan had been completed. In the last two singles groups yesterday, the United States unexpectedly defeated Japan, winning the rematch rights by a score of three to two. The American overseas Chinese in the venue were all relieved. After the United States broke through the first difficult hurdle, they were confident in meeting Great Britain in the rematch and it was not difficult to win the finals. The remaining doubles matches between Great Britain and Switzerland ended with Great Britain winning three to zero. The doubles matches between Portugal and Germany also ended with Portugal winning three to zero. Great Britain and Portugal have already won two singles groups and one doubles group, and have all won the rematch rights. As for the results of the remaining two doubles groups, they are not important. The situation of each group yesterday is described below.

United States Wins Two Singles Matches Against Japan 109

Scuria Wins Over Machida: The Japanese player Machida is a famous player on the sea, and his forehand topspin and overhead smash are his specialties. He is the mainstay of the Japanese team this time. In the first two singles matches, he defeated the American McIsaac Smith with three straight wins, but yesterday he lost to the American Scuria by a score of one to three. The two sides fought fiercely, and both sides were exhausted at the end of the match. Machida was dejected, and the Japanese overseas Chinese were very disappointed. In contrast, Scuria was very proud, and the people of his country competed to shake hands with him, and he was extraordinary.

In the first set, Scuria took the lead and gained two games, creating a strong momentum. Machida was not willing to be outdone and tried hard to fight, using all his topspin skills. The score was tied at four and five games each. Scuria was inspired and won the next game, winning by a score of seven to five.

In the second set, although Scuria once held the most advantageous position with a score of three to one, Machida's spirit suddenly increased and his ball power was very strong. The strong and good-fighting Scuria was unconsciously eclipsed and was exhausted. Machida returned a set by a score of six to three.

In the third set, the American army always had the upper hand and never lost three, so it won again by a score of six to three.

The fourth set was of great importance, and the Japanese army tried hard to retaliate, gaining two games first and showing great promise. Scuria was strong-willed and persevering. He was able to create four consecutive games after losing by two to three, reversing the defeat and winning by a score of six to three, winning the audience's applause.

The two sides had similar physiques and similar hitting methods. Each side had a good performance, which aroused the audience's great interest. Scuria's serve was very skilled and he was able to persevere and fight calmly, so there were few mistakes, which was the reason for his victory.

(US) Scuria 7 5 3 6 6 3 6 3 Machida (Japan)

Smithke and Kitao: In the previous two German singles, the Japanese Kitao lost to the American Scuria, and the American Smith lost to the Japanese Machida. Therefore, both Smith and Kitao were losers, but the relationship between the gains and losses of both sides was not light, so they had to do their best to fight. Smith's attitude was very calm, and his ball was never empty. His serving skills could be compared with the German Scuria. Both used long guns to challenge. Smith attacked in the east and west, leaving Kitao no time to run. As a result, Smith won by a score of three to zero. Comparing Smith's skills yesterday with the battle against Machida the other day, they were like two different people. The comparison is as follows:

(US) Smith 6 2 6 3 6 3 Kitao (Japan)

Portugal Defeats Germany in Doubles 110

In yesterday's doubles match between Portugal and Germany, the Portuguese players were Carvalho and S. Korasha, while Germany still fielded Crowe and Ibert, the singles players from the other day. In comparison, Germany's strength was far inferior. The German player, Ibert, was very portly and obese, weighing at least two hundred forty or fifty pounds. He could neither run nor bend, but his hitting technique was quite good; he could calmly hit the ball when it came near him, which was not easy. As a result, Portugal won three sets in a row.

(Portugal) Carvalho S. Korasha 63 62 61 Crowe Ibert (Germany)

England Defeats Switzerland in Doubles 111

Yesterday's doubles match between England and Switzerland also resulted in a victory for England. England had veteran White and George pairing up, with ample fighting strength. Switzerland still fielded Atdot and White Instruments. The match was decided in three sets, with the total number of games being 21. Switzerland only won three games. The comparison is as follows:

(England) White George 61 62 60 Atdot White Instruments (Switzerland)

In the preliminary rounds, the United States defeated Japan 3-2, England defeated Switzerland 3-0, and Portugal defeated Germany 3-0, all securing spots in the semi-finals. Although England, Switzerland, Portugal, and Germany each have two singles matches remaining, the outcomes are irrelevant, so they will not be held today. The semi-final schedule is as follows: the United States vs. England, and China vs. Portugal, starting on the 21st.

Chen Jianxiao, Director of the Ministry of Education, Resigns 112

To Take a Professorship at National Wuhan University

Chen Jianxiao, Director of the Social Education Department and concurrently Director of the Mongolian Education Department of the Ministry of Education, has served for two and a half years since taking office. He has always been diligent and devoted to his duties. However, Mr. Chen is a specialized scholar and is not accustomed to administrative life, so he has long held the intention to resign. Recently, in response to an invitation from National Wuhan University to serve as a professor in psychology and education, he specifically requested Minister Jiang to resign. It is also heard that he left Beijing for Hangzhou yesterday with his family, expressing his firm intention to resign.

Ministry of Education Commends the Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Education for Supplementary Readers for Lower Grades of Elementary School 113

The Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Education organized an editorial committee for supplementary readers for the lower grades of elementary school last year, separately compiling various supplementary readers for the lower grades of elementary school. Ten types of supplementary readers for revolutionary memorial festivals have been compiled. After detailed review and the addition of illustrations, they were submitted to the Ministry of Education for review and approval. Yesterday, Directive No. 1890 of the Ministry of Education was received, stating briefly that the submitted books have now been reviewed by the Ministry. After examining the content, the selection of materials is able to meet the needs of children, and the illustrations are also precise. The bureau's guidance work for schools is quite diligent and worthy of commendation. The ten types of supplementary readers have been slightly revised in accordance with the instructions issued by the Ministry of Education and will be printed and used soon.

Letter to the Editor Dear Editor, In the education column of your newspaper on the 17th, there was a piece about the turmoil at Fudan Practical Middle School. This news was the result of a conversation with a certain old classmate from Fudan University and is not directly related to the problems of our school or clear about the circumstances of this incident. The motive for the organization of the faculty and staff school protection association of our school is to maintain the dignity of the education community and the excellent and special spirit of our school, as well as the autonomy stipulated in the contract between our school and the university. All actions are based on these reasons. Our school has now been officially taken over by Mr. Li Baohuan, according to the resolution of the general meeting of all faculty and staff last semester, in conjunction with the school protection association, and all important school documents, including contracts and seals, are fully kept. On the one hand, Director Chen Wangdao is requested to return to school to handle affairs after his leave. Before Director Chen agrees to return to school, fortunately, Mr. Li is responsible for all school affairs and invites all faculty and staff to work hard to maintain normal operations so as not to cause disputes and suspension. This is the situation of our school's dispute. As for the detailed situation, it can be found in our school's ten-day publication and the two declarations of the school protection association. This letter is hereby sent for your peace of mind. Sincerely, Fudan Experimental Middle School August 17th
