Xu Meizhen's Repentance Marriage Record 181

The childhood marriage contract was not agreed to, and the fiancé fled without any guilt.

Xu Meizhen, a woman from Zhangjiangzha, Pudong, father Chuanjiang works as a typecaster in the printing bureau, brother Jinzhang works as a typesetter in the Commercial Press. When Meizhen was eight years old, her father died of illness. When he was alive, Lu Deru and others matched Meizhen to Tang Pinmei's son. Unfortunately, Tang's son died of illness, and Meizhen became a widow (commonly known as a door-viewing widow). Later, her brother Jinzhang acted as the master, and Xi Liushi, Shen Meisheng and others acted as matchmakers. In the ninth year of the Republic of China, she was betrothed to Xi Qiren, the son of Xi Zhushu, a man from the 23rd Tu of the 20th Bao in Yuancheng City. At the time of the engagement, Meizhen was eleven years old and Qiren was nine years old. They were innocent and played with each other every day. Zhushu saw that his daughter-in-law was lively and smart, and he loved her very much. Zhushu was a member of the education circle with a new mind. He liked to read books and saw that the woman's family was poor and unable to cultivate her. He then started the Yuyu Primary School in his hometown and sent her to school. After more than three years, he changed to Yiguang Girls' School in Chuansha. The expenses for study, meals, books, and clothing were all fully borne by Zhushu (at that time, the woman's brother Jinzhang had died). In the third year after Meizhen entered school, Zhushu died of illness, and the tuition fees were not available, so she dropped out of school. Not long after, because the family situation was not as difficult as before, she changed to Zhangjiang School to study, and then changed to Nanhui Girls' Middle School. At that time, Xi Qiren was learning typesetting in Shanghai Xingye Sample Making Shop. His mother thought that Qiren was already a young man and his daughter-in-law had grown up. She planned to choose the 16th day of the first month of the next year of the abolished calendar to get married. On the 19th and 20th of May of this year, she invited the matchmaker twice to notify and replenish the festival ceremony. Unexpectedly, Meizhen and others scolded and refused to accept it. Xi Soshi (Qiren's mother) had no way to think about it, so she filed a lawsuit. On the day before yesterday, the Nanhui County Government summoned both parties to court. According to the matchmaker Xi Liushi, the Xu family had received 20 yuan for the engagement money and a gold hair clip. The Xu family was responsible for the reading and cultivation. The Xi family's engagement money was 60 yuan and the fees for Meizhen's childhood reading, etc., were not the case. Xi Soshi briefly supplied that her son Qiren suddenly disappeared due to the stimulation of this divorce. She searched everywhere and could not find him, so she did not appear in court. She could not agree to the termination of the marriage contract. Xu Liushi (Meizhen's mother) said that she could not be the master of the marriage contract and had to ask her daughter Xu Meizhen. Meizhen supplied that she absolutely requested the termination of the marriage contract. She asked Xi Qiren because he was stimulated and fled. If he committed suicide because of frustration in love, would you be able to live with him? She replied that I and him had been engaged since childhood, and I did not agree to it. There will never be a good feeling in the future. If he commits suicide, it has nothing to do with me. Moreover, the divorce is now stipulated in the party constitution of married people. It is absolutely free, let alone unmarried officials. Although the reasons for your request to terminate the marriage contract are very sufficient, it is inevitable that you are too thin in human relations. The interrogation was announced to be over and the debate was over, and both parties left.

Health Bureau Approves Sale of Second-Class Meat 183

Inferior to Wholly Healthy Livestock Meat

Shanghai Municipal Health Bureau Announcement: This announcement concerns the fact that the purpose of the Bureau's livestock inspection is to prevent the sale of meat from plague-ridden animals under false pretenses, thereby protecting the health of citizens. Subsequently, if pigs, cattle, or sheep are found to have localized diseases, the diseased parts will still be removed, and the remaining parts will be stamped with a blue "Approved" mark. However, the stamp will also include the characters "Second Class" to indicate that the meat comes from pigs, cattle, or sheep that are not entirely disease-free. Although it is permissible to sell such meat for consumption, its quality is ultimately inferior to that of meat from completely healthy livestock, allowing citizens to make informed choices when purchasing. This announcement is hereby promulgated for public awareness. August 16th, Nineteenth Year of the Republic of China. Director: Hu Hongji.

Wang Hua, a 53-year-old woman from Wuxi, currently lives at number 32, Xihuaqinfang, Zhoujiaqiao, Shanghai. She lost her husband early and relied on working in a yarn factory for a living. She gave birth to a son named Jingbao, who is now 21 years old, and raised him with difficulty. She asked someone to help him get a job at the Shenxin Yarn Factory. At first, he was quite frugal, so his mother loved him especially because he was her only son. A few years ago, she hired a Ding woman to marry her son. His mother, because she was old and weak, was planning to rely on her son and daughter-in-law to spend her remaining years. Unexpectedly, her son Jingbao suddenly changed his ways since last year and no longer engaged in proper employment, specializing in associating with rogues, roaming and gambling. Despite repeated persuasion from his mother and wife, it was ineffective. The clothes in the house were pawned by him. Recently, it has become even more absurd. Not only does he not care for his mother and wife, but he also occasionally mistreats his old mother and beats his wife for no reason. At about 6:00 p.m. the day before yesterday, Jingbao returned home and demanded money from his mother, and she kept pestering her. When she did not get what she wanted, she cursed her mother and almost beat her. The mother could no longer endure and immediately called the police to come and arrest the rebellious son and take him back to the Sixth District Police Station. After questioning by District Chief Ren, it was determined that the crime of the case was unfilial to his old mother and that he could not be excused. Yesterday, a document was prepared and he was sent to the local court for trial.

The Husband is Unscrupulous 193

Chopping at Wife's Head with a Cleaver

Wang Gu, a woman from Yancheng in her forties, lives on a boat in Tanziwan, Zhabei. Her husband, Wang Wencai, has been married for many years and has been harmonious. However, Wang now has another affair and often lingers outside for days without returning home, neglecting his family. Yesterday, Wang earned twenty-two dollars and eight cents from a counting job, and Gu asked him for two dollars to buy tung oil to coat the boat. But at this time, Wang Wencai regarded his wife as an enemy and refused to give her a penny. Gu, feeling that her husband was so ruthless, refused to give up and rushed forward to hug his feet and cry. Unexpectedly, this provoked Wang's anger, and he grabbed the cleaver on the table and chopped at Gu's head, causing blood to flow like a fountain. A crowd of neighbors gathered, all speaking out for her injustice. They immediately called a patrol officer from another post to arrest Wang and take him to the third squadron of the police and then to the fourth district headquarters. After questioning by Director Jin, it was determined that the case was related to abuse of his wife, and he was ordered to be sent to the bureau for questioning.

The Villainous Scheme of Thugs at the Wharf 194

Swapping Fake Silver Coins with Plaster

Recently, at the wharves along the Huangpu River from the Ningshao Wharf, Dada Wharf, to the New Wharf in Nanshi, there has been a group of vagrants disguised as rickshaw pullers and porters, mingling in the crowd. When ships arrive and passengers disembark, they pretend to carry goods and transport luggage, and then take the opportunity to steal luggage and miscellaneous items. When passengers who have had their goods carried ashore pay the porters, they use their deceptive means to falsely claim that the silver coins paid are not good and forcibly swap them. They then use lead or copper coins to exchange for silver coins. Or after being noticed by passengers, a search of their bodies also finds no conclusive evidence, and they can only pay the price. In fact, these people first put the fake silver coins in the largest plaster and stick it on their bodies. Whenever passengers pay, they have already taken out the fake silver coins from the plaster without being prepared. After the good silver coins are hidden, they strongly swap the fake coins. As a result, there are countless victims among the travelers. Their skills are extremely cunning, so although Chen Youhua, the district chief of the first district in charge, has sent police to investigate in various places for days and has been quite strict, he has not yet made any arrests.

Daughter-in-Law Commits Suicide by Poisoning after Argument with Mother-in-Law 195

Wang Chunbo, a native of Yangzhou, opened a Xinhua Copperware and Electric Light Shop at 4 Houpi Lane, Baoxingli, French Concession. He married Xu, a woman from the same hometown (29 years old), as his wife. The relationship between the couple was still strong, but there were often quarrels between the mother-in-law and daughter-in-law. The day before yesterday, there was another dispute over trivial matters, and Xu suddenly had a suicidal thought. She secretly took poison and committed suicide at 10:00 a.m. At 3:00 p.m., she had a poison attack. Her husband learned of it and sent her to Renji Hospital for treatment. Because she was too poisoned, the treatment was ineffective and she died in the hospital at 5:00 a.m. yesterday. The hospital notified the police to order detectives to carry the body to the Tongren Fuyuanyuan Hall for an autopsy. Zhu, the presiding judge of the Criminal Section of the French Police, came to the hall at 11:00 a.m. to inspect the body. He first sat in the public seat and had the bailiff report the previous situation. After Mr. Zhu questioned the husband of the deceased, he ordered that Wang Xu had indeed died of her own will due to some reason before her death. The police were ordered to select a Western doctor to examine the body and submit a report. After the examination, Wang Chunbo, the husband of the deceased, was allowed to prepare a coffin for burial.

Two People Died from Electric Shock 196

Liu Yinlong, a tea customer at the Tongfuyuan Teahouse at 562 Xiaoshadu Road in Shanghai, suddenly had a broken electric wire at about 7:00 p.m. the day before yesterday, and all the lights went out. Liu Yinlong, who claimed to be good at repairing, started working. Occasionally, he accidentally touched the electric wire with his finger and fell to the ground. By the time he was sent to the hospital, the electricity had already attacked his heart, and it was too late for treatment, so he died. After receiving the report, the police sent detectives to carry the body to the autopsy hall on Feilun Road. Yesterday morning, Xu, a prosecutor from the Special District Local Court, came to the hall to investigate and confirmed that it was a fatal electric shock. Shao Jiu, the director of the teahouse, felt deeply sorry for Liu's sacrifice for repairing the lights for his shop and agreed to give Liu Li, the wife of the deceased, 80 yuan per year for five consecutive years and signed a contract. So he accompanied the wife of the deceased to the case to explain the process. Prosecutor Xu then ordered the woman to sign and receive the body for burial.

Shen Yinfathe, an apprentice at a electric light repair shop at 576 Beijing Road, Shen Yinfa, was only 17 years old. At 8:45 p.m. the night before last, he was repairing an electric fan in the shop. However, his skills were still immature, so he was shocked and the shop owner sent him to Renji Hospital by car. But it was too late to save him and he died soon after. The Laozha Police Station, after receiving the report, sent detectives to carry the body to the autopsy hall on Feilun Road. Yesterday morning, Prosecutor Xu from the Special District Local Court came to the hall to inspect and ordered the brother of the deceased, Shen Jinxiang, to sign and receive the body for burial.

Female Guest Lodges, Money Missing 197

Zhang Chu Accuses Song Liqing

Zhang Chu, a 44-year-old woman from Nanhui, has been living in her hometown. The day before yesterday, she came to Shanghai with her 25-year-old son, Weibin, to stay at the Taian Inn at Wangjia Wharf in Nanshi, intending to take a boat to Ningbo the next day. After spending a night, she prepared to leave yesterday morning and checked her luggage one by one. Unexpectedly, more than one hundred dollars stored in the rattan basket suddenly disappeared. In a hurry, she asked the waiter, who claimed not to know. Later, she twisted the inn owner Song Liqing to the first district station for investigation and requested investigation. It was ordered to wait for the warden to conduct a preliminary review and handle it.

Man Throws Himself into the River, Speaks Incoherently 198

Appears to Suffer from Mental Illness

Yesterday afternoon at 1:00 p.m., a middle-aged man resembling a coolie suddenly threw himself into the Huangpu River at Pengjia Wharf in Landidu, Pudong. Fortunately, he was rescued by a boatman and handed over to the post police, who took him to the third district for questioning. He claimed that his name was Zhang Aba, 31 years old, from Danyang, living in Huangjiagou, Pudong, working as a handyman. The act of jumping into the river was because Guanyin Bodhisattva called him to wash his body so that he could ascend to heaven. He also said that no one should ask any more questions, otherwise he would report to the authorities. District Chief Zhang considered that his words were incoherent and seemed to be insane. He could not reason with him, so he ordered the police to inform his wife, Leng, to take her husband back and monitor his actions to prevent a second suicide.

Woman Sues Stepmother for Inheritance 199

Jurisdictional Issues Still to Be Resolved

A Liu from Hangzhou moved with his family to Rixinli, Duntu Road in Shanghai. Later, he returned to Hangzhou for medical treatment and died in his residence on Huashi Street in Hangzhou. The estate of more than 50,000 yuan was all in his hometown. However, his wife and old mother are still living in Shanghai. A daughter named Liu Qiang, who is at the age of a flower, lives in Zhongwang Lane 214, Ningbo Road. She has a new style of short hair fashion. Now, because a daughter also has the right to inherit the estate, she has hired a lawyer to file a lawsuit against her stepmother, Liu Li, for the division of the estate. The case opened at the Special District Local Court yesterday morning by Judge Xu Wenrong. The defendant, Liu Li, did not arrive and only sent a letter to the court in advance stating that her address was in Hangzhou, which was not under the jurisdiction of the concession court. Liu Qiang claimed that the defendant often traveled between Hangzhou and Shanghai, and that her grandmother was still living in Shanghai. She also submitted a list of the estate as evidence, saying that she now requested to divide the estate equally with her brother. After reviewing it, Judge Xu considered that the property listed in the list was all located in the Zhejiang area, and the person being inherited had died in Hangzhou. The case should be conducted in Hangzhou for convenience. The plaintiff's lawyer argued that it should be resolved in Shanghai. Judge Xu then ordered a change of date to investigate the jurisdictional issues clearly before proceeding.

Yesterday afternoon at 4:00 p.m., Mr. Zhang Zhijiang and several martial arts colleagues visited the Kang Yuan Flower Iron Printing and Can Making Factory on Huade Road. The late Prime Minister wanted to restore the original morals of the Chinese people, so moral cultivation should be the beginning. Everyone should strictly observe the factory regulations and receive true factory training to cultivate morals. (2) Physical exercise, divided into labor and exercise. The factory is a place of labor. Everyone should work hard and tirelessly during work hours to embody the true meaning of exercise. More importantly, they should practice martial arts. First, it can preserve the national essence and promote the national glory. Second, it can strengthen the body and strengthen the race, fundamentally saving the country. Third, it can resist foreign aggression and avenge national humiliation. Fourth, it can self-hygiene and survival. After the speech, Mr. Xiang gave a speech briefly saying that listening to Mr. Zhang's experienced words is better than reading ten years of books. He deeply hoped that colleagues would realize and implement every sentence in order to live up to Mr. Zhang and their own ears. Next, martial arts colleagues performed martial arts on the spot. The employees and students of the dragon swimming and tiger leaping Qi Wan Shen were full of admiration. It is heard that Mr. Xiang准 has invited Mr. Zhang to send a martial arts expert to train the factory's employees and students. Mr. Zhang has agreed. Before leaving, he personally wrote on the factory's equipment organization. It is really rare to see such precision and completeness. I admire it very much. A few words in the factory's guest instruction book and everyone parted happily.

Debt Control Case of Jingcheng Resolved Through Reconciliation 201

Jingcheng Paper Company previously issued industrial bonds in the name of promoting business. The articles of association stipulate that the weekly interest rate is one point and dividends can be distributed. It plans to raise a total of 200,000 yuan of debt and return 50,000 yuan each year to be cleared in four years. Unexpectedly, after obtaining the funds, it neither expanded its business nor fulfilled the charter of drawing lots to repay the principal. Therefore, the bondholder Liu Ziwei hired lawyers Yang Guoshu to sue Wang Shuxian, the general manager of the company, in the Special District Local Court. The case has been summoned for trial once and ordered to resolve outside the court. The previous newspaper has reported it. It is now known that the two parties have peacefully resolved the matter outside the court. The method is that the defendant will first pay the interest of 1,800 yuan, and the owed bond of 9,000 yuan will be returned in five months. Yesterday morning, the defendant's agent lawyer, Lin Yingqing, brought 1,800 yuan in cash to the court and handed it over to the plaintiff's lawyer, Yang Guoshu, for counting. He then explained the reconciliation situation and the proposed conditions. After Judge Xu ordered the clerk to make a reconciliation record, the lawyers of both parties signed the case.

Songhu Branch Line Ticket Supplementation Revised 205

50% Additional Charge to Ticket Price

The regulations for supplementing tickets on the Songhu Branch Line of the Beijing-Shanghai Railway used to be calculated by doubling the ticket price. It is now revised to stipulate that from today onwards, the regulations for supplementing tickets on the branch line will charge an additional 50% in addition to the ticket price. The supplemental ticket fee will be calculated as 5 cents for those less than 5 cents, and 1 dime for those less than 1 dime. The Railway Bureau has notified all ticket inspectors to follow.

Letter 207

To the Editor: I was surprised to read in your newspaper on the 13th of this month that I lost a check due to lack of wedding expenses and committed suicide by throwing myself into the river. I was ordered by my boss to go to the countryside on the 18th of last month to collect debts. I did not receive a check for one hundred taels of silver until the beginning of this month, and I planned to return to Shanghai to report back to my boss. Unexpectedly, I suddenly felt weak and had diarrhea. I sought medical treatment and have not yet recovered. I immediately sent a letter to my younger brother, Ji Yue, to inform my boss about the check. As for the so-called suicide note, it is even more fabricated. I think someone is holding a grudge and intentionally damaging my reputation. This kind of rumor is completely inconsistent with the facts. Since my reputation is at stake, please check and correct it to match the facts. Sincerely, Cai Duming, 86.

Social News

Large Number of Americans Traveling Abroad 208

One in Ten Travels to Canada

New York News: Americans are known for their fondness for traveling abroad. Not to mention those who go to Europe, the total amount of money spent by American tourists in Canada in the previous year actually reached 600 million yuan. The number of cars crossing the border was about 4.5 million, with an average of three people per car, totaling 13 million people, which means that one in ten Americans travels to Canada. In addition, there are also a considerable number of people who travel by train and ship. Also, judging from the number of cars alone, there were 800,000 more last year than the previous year, and the number is gradually increasing. Also, because alcohol is prohibited in the United States, a large number of people cross the border to buy and drink.

Revenue of South Manchuria Railway Decreases 209

6 Million Yuan Decrease from April to July

World News Agency reports, according to Japanese sources, that the South Manchuria Railway has been affected by the sluggish world market and its business performance is currently sluggish. The revenue has decreased by 6 million yuan compared to the previous year. In addition, the transportation of special products has decreased and coal prices have plummeted, making the situation quite difficult. If this trend continues, it may be necessary to reduce interest distribution in the next period.

Plants Possess Morality 210

According to discoveries by biologists, all plants not only breathe but also have a circulatory system through which their life fluids flow, just like animals. Recently, scientists have discovered that some plants possess morality. For example, there is licorice in India, the petals of which are extremely sensitive to changes in climate and can predict storms, earthquakes, and volcanic eruptions. There is also a plant called the compass plant, whose petals and leaf tips always point north and can serve as a compass for those lost. There is also a parasitic grass that clings to other trees year-round, absorbing their sap, but when the leaves of the host tree wither in the harsh winter, the grass returns the nutrients it absorbed in the spring and summer to the trunk of the host tree. There is also an orchid that grows on trees but obtains its nutrients from the air, never taking anything from the tree it parasitizes, and in return for the favor of shelter, it is willing to use its beautiful self as an ornament for the tree's leaves. However, there are also extremely immoral plants that specialize in preying on their own kind and insects. The most ferocious of these is called the Venus Fly Trap. Its two leaves form a beautiful cup surrounded by floral whiskers. Inside, it stores fragrant juice to lure insects. When an insect touches its whiskers, the leaf cup closes and traps it. There is also an aquatic plant called Bladderwort, which uses the same method to capture aquatic insects and small fish. Another is the Madagascar Pitcher, which can use its twin leaves to capture fairly large rats, and its nature is particularly cruel. Inside its leaf trap, there are extremely fine sharp thorns to stab its captives to death and eat them.

Joint Transportation Commences This Month on Five Railways in the Eastern Provinces 213

According to the World News Agency, Tokyo reports that a joint transportation conference was held in Shenyang in mid-July by the Beining, Sitao, Taoang, and Qikesi Railways. It was decided that there would be one round-trip passenger train per day between Beiping and Dahushan, between Tongliao and Zhengjiatun, between Zhengjiatun and Taonan, and between Taonan and Ang'angxi. The maximum waiting time at interchange points between sections would be one hour. Furthermore, the Shenhai and Jihai lines will also open to traffic on August 1. While this matter appears on the surface to be merely a matter of business negotiations between Chinese railways, it is in fact a measure taken by the Dongsan Provinces government to implement its policy toward the South Manchuria Railway. The Japanese government is paying close attention to this recent development. Regarding the implementation of this joint transportation, it has recently been learned that the Northeast Political Affairs Committee, the administrative body of the Dongsan Provinces government, has decided to reduce railway freight rates in various provinces, with the intention of attracting passengers and goods from the South Manchuria Railway and substantially recovering the benefits of the South Manchuria Railway. Therefore, instructions and announcements are being issued to the general public to ensure a thorough understanding of this intention.

Page 19

Book and Newspaper Introductions

War 217

— Guang Mei

Politics can influence literature and art, and literature and art can influence politics. Certain political conditions can produce certain forms of literature and art, and the construction of certain literature and art can create certain political conditions. The two have a mutual relationship that cannot be separated. At the same time, literature and art are products of a nation, the crystallization of the nation's development process. In other words, literature and art belong to the nation, which cannot be denied.

In literature and art, opposing war has become fashionable. They believe that as long as nations exist in the world, war is inevitable. They consider all wars to be evil and that the only way to eliminate wars between nations is through class struggle. I do not understand this view. When the Japanese killed the worker Gu Zhenghong during the May Thirtieth Incident, why did a group of students rise up to support him, disregarding everything to form a procession on Nanjing Road and give speeches, resulting in such a shocking and bloody tragedy? All Chinese people, no matter how deeply they were asleep, were completely awakened by this and were all agitated and excited. At this time, compatriots across the country responded unanimously, and all who heard it were outraged. As a result, support associations sprang up everywhere, raising donations to help the striking compatriots. People who were usually extremely frugal were willing to donate generously. If class consciousness were more important than national consciousness, why would the Chinese people have risen up in such a unified movement? And why would the so-called bourgeoisie in China not help the Japanese capitalists who killed Gu Zhenghong to oppress the Chinese laborers, but instead help the Chinese laborers to resist the Japanese capitalists? At the same time, why would the laborers of Japan or other countries not rise up to help the Chinese laborers to resist the Japanese capitalists? All Chinese people, including scholars, farmers, workers, merchants, and government officials, rose up in a unified movement. What is the reason for this? Furthermore, recently, when the Great Light Theater premiered, Hong Shen, unafraid of death, saw it and considered it an insult to the Chinese nation. The film depicted Chinese people selling opium and committing theft in foreign countries, but it did not specify that these were done by university professors or so-called intellectuals. Since those ugly deeds had nothing to do with Hong Shen, why did he impatiently begin to lecture, demanding that the theater owner refund the tickets? When this case was heard in court, the audience was particularly large and excited, causing a nationwide sensation. Telegrams from all provinces and cities could be read in the newspapers. Such matters, which had nothing to do with Hong Shen's personal pain or with the Chinese intellectual class, caused Hong Shen to go crazy, and why did the whole country follow him in his madness? What is the reason for this?

Under such simple and obvious circumstances, the so-called importance of class consciousness over national consciousness is naturally self-defeating.

Here, a long-unresolved problem arises. This problem is the issue of nationalism and war. Recently, I read Mr. Dickinson's article "War" in the seventh issue of "The Vanguard Weekly," which explains the war problem that we have long wanted to resolve but could not, in a thorough and vivid manner. Now, I excerpt the most poignant sections below:

Regarding war, whether domestic or foreign, we should recognize its nature. There are wars of imperialism invading other nations or countries, wars of nations seeking independence and freedom, wars of countries seeking independence and freedom, wars of domestic warlord separatism, and wars of party banditry. We should undoubtedly make every effort to attack feudal separatism, imperialism, and party wars. In the pursuit of national freedom and independence, when a nation resists foreign aggression, this mutual conflict is a just resistance and a just advancement. If the Chinese nation wants to achieve its goal of independence and freedom, it must first eliminate all imperialist, warlord, and party aggression and oppression. To eliminate this aggression, plunder, and oppression, and to achieve independence and freedom, we must pay the price with our strength and blood. We firmly believe that national independence and freedom can only be exchanged for strength and blood, and that national humiliation can only be washed away with strength and blood. In order to awaken the national consciousness, we should use the power of literature and art to depict, express, and eternally engrave on the hearts of the general public and eternally infuse into the blood of the general public all the moving, admirable, inspiring, and touching deeds of all wars for national independence and freedom, so that they know that this kind of war should be commemorated and celebrated.

The problem that we have long wanted to solve but could not has thus been resolved very thoroughly.

"The Vanguard Weekly," Issue 9, Published

"The Vanguard Weekly," Issue 9, published by "The Vanguard Society," was published yesterday. The main articles include: Ye Qiuyuan's "The Theoretical Foundation of Nationalist Literature and Art" (continued); Li Yi's "Arise" (poem); Tan Feng, Jia Zemin's "Two Kinds of National Essence," Yi, Guo Moruo's "Oracle Bone Inscriptions," Bing, Ma Yangren's translation of Ding, Muren's play and Zheng Boze's "Two Orphans" (continued). Sales locations include: in this city, the Kaiming, Modern, Guanghua, Zhenmeishan, Jinwu, and New Life bookstores; and in other cities, major bookstores.

Selected Poems 218

— Tang Zengyang

"The Short Story Monthly," April Issue

The most typical and artistic poetry has been silent for a long time in the seemingly weak Chinese literary world. If it is to be revived, it contains infinite hope and will happen soon. Because, with our keen eyes, we observe the Chinese literary world, and the highest artistic expression of poetry is full of the phenomenon of re-emerging. Moreover, its content and form are different from the poems created by scholars who vigorously advocated the literary movement of the May Fourth era. They are completely different. This is probably because modern poets have a deeper understanding and are more cautious when writing poetry, washing away the strange phenomena of the past poetry world, the so-called style of crude production. At the same time, the authorities in the literary world are particularly strict in selecting poetry, simply using another eye to appreciate this poetry that reveals true feelings, thus raising the inherent value of poetry.

To know that the most beautiful flower to expect for the re-opening of poetry is of course to see the efforts of the so-called young poets who are slightly cultivated. Each poem only seeks qualitative fulfillment and refinement. In terms of quantity, I hope it is not as good as the crude production of the May Fourth era, but most of the power can be said to be the lifeline of the revival of poetry, which still relies on the current sincere advocates who are in charge of the literary world, just like in the Western poetry world. At the same time, there must be loyal critics to emerge.

In the past two years, "The Short Story Monthly" has not published poetry. The April issue of the recently published "The Short Story Monthly" suddenly discovered the poetry selection column before the creation, including six original poems and one translated poem, which is a surprising surprise to those of us who have a great taste for poetry.

In fact, what we need now is poetry that belongs to nationalism. What is full of decadent colors, sad cries, violent calls, romantic words, etc. as the content of poetry is not needed in the near future, nor is it absolutely not needed in the future. In other words, what is urgently hoped to be produced at present is poetry that greatly expresses the Chinese nation, moving forward, upward, fighting for freedom and prosperity. Of course, there are still people working hard in this direction. Several of the poems published in the recent "The Short Story Monthly" are creations full of national consciousness, even Zheng Zhenduo's translated poem "The Death of a Knight" is like this. Now, I will introduce them separately below.

Liu Yanling's "The Sky" is a narrative poem of nearly one hundred lines, using May, which has the most national humiliation memorial days, as the background of the whole poem. Because of this piercing May, it reminds us of Japan's aggression against China, the various misfortunes of the two boils on the fingertips of Lushun, etc. At the same time, the author also holds a passionate hope for China, urging the youth who are still lingering in their dreams. In his poems, it can be seen very clearly:

Scene after scene, we remember clearly, as clear as the face of Mount Fuji. China is a tender green leaf, you are like an insect, always running it. China is a beautiful and clean young man, who was mistaken for your powdery and greasy fragrance and took off his clothes to see his skin. Heaven knows the sores and scars behind it.

We can understand how enthusiastic and deeply nationalistic the author's mood was when writing, filled with words that can arouse the reader's sincere love for China, and make people feel how unbeautiful it is that such a beautiful and clean young man has so many sores and scars on his body, and how should we heal these wounds and restore the true face of the past? I believe that readers who have read the two sections of poems quoted above are at least deeply imprinted with such a general concept. Indeed, poetry is the highest expression of emotion in art, and it can move people's hearts and be so profound and powerful.

Winter rests, all life droops, and dead leaves carry on hand in hand, which means that if we work hard like this, what national humiliation will not be cleared away? The germination of all kinds of flowers in spring implies the future prosperous national destiny, but their deep and secret intentions are not as piercing as the heart in May.

This is true. How painful it is to remember all our national humiliations. If we unite and work hard for the country, the national humiliation will eventually be cleared away. We should also know that our Chinese nation contains unlimited hope in the future, just like the germination of all kinds of flowers in spring, full of green vitality. We Chinese people must remember this May, which has supreme wounds, in its entirety. The author's symbolism is also very strong. Let's look at the ending of his poem:

Wave after wave, another wave of memories drips until dawn. Sisters and brothers, don't sleep, listen forever, hear until dawn every night.

The author of Zheng Zhenduo's translated poem "The Death of a Knight" is unknown. According to the translator's note, this poem was translated several years ago, but it has been forgotten in the pile of books until now, and the author of the original poem and the original book it came from have also been forgotten. Because it is exciting and gratifying, it is specially taken out and published here. This is of course a regret, but it is only good if the content of the poem is particularly full and exciting, and this poem is full of very deep national ideas. It is strange that the translator's note did not remind him of this point.

I drink the first glass of wine, holding a knife, for him, for the people who died for the motherland, drink this glass. Now quickly drink the second glass, this will be drunk for freedom, and then the enemies of freedom will have to escape.

My love, the cup is empty, the bullets are ringing, the rider is shouting, there is no time to drink and sing anymore. Come, break the cup, and my love will go to the enemy. There is no death more joyful than this.

The whole poem is rich in very deep national central ideas. Because of the length of this publication, the whole poem could not be quoted here, which is a pity. When general poetry writers read this translated poem, I really don't know how to work hard. At the same time, I hope that the translator will introduce more of this type of poem.

Rules for Book and Newspaper Introduction Articles 219

(1) The text is limited to introducing the latest publications at home and abroad. In addition to literary works, all political, economic, legal, scientific, and educational books and newspapers are included in the introduction. However, boring books and newspapers will not be introduced.

(2) The pictures are limited to the recent works of new domestic and foreign artists and illustrations related to the text.

(3) Articles on textual research or research on ancient Chinese books will not be published.

(4) Pictures and photos are limited to those related to the text.

(5) Each article should not exceed 3,000 characters.

(6) Do not write on both sides of the manuscript paper.

(7) Do not write the manuscript horizontally. Do not write carelessly. Western text can be omitted if possible. If it is necessary to quote the original text, it must be attached below the translation.

Theater News 220

The Bai Xing Grand Theater proclaims that the theater is currently showing the world-renowned director Mu Niu Ai's masterpiece, "The Four Great Heavenly Kings," plus the calm and sorrowful performances of the four great stars, including Jeanne Gaynor. It's wonderful and a must-see.

Business News 221

Huaxin Company on Nanjing Road declares that the company will hold an autumn sale starting on the 18th of this month for 25 days, with all mass-market goods reduced by 70% to 90%. Seasonal new styles of silk yarn clothing and men's and women's white leather shoes are especially cheap. In order to promote domestic products, silk stockings, handkerchiefs, and towels from major Chinese factories are sold at cost. Although gold prices are high for other Western-style products, such as suits, undershirts, cosmetics, and fragrances, they can only be sold at the old low prices due to large inventories.

The general distribution office of Anlu Cotton Weaving Factory on Nanjing Road proclaims that the new building produced by the factory opened yesterday, and customers were crowded upstairs and downstairs. More than 2,000 dozen Eye brand towels were sold, and bed sheets, bathrobes, and towel quilts were almost sold out. The shirts manufactured by the factory are managed and supervised by experts and have special characteristics. The patterns in the fabric department on the second floor are also quite complete.

Guan Shengyuan proclaims that the company, which is famous for making scientific oven-baked mooncakes, is approaching the new autumn season and must immediately manufacture mooncakes. Based on past experience, the company has improved its manufacturing process. It is said that the recent products include various types such as bean paste, bean puree, five kernels, sweet meat, salty meat, golden leg, and lotus seed paste, which are still sold at the original price, ranging from 17 cents to 23 cents per piece. The taste has been improved compared to last year. The head office of the Japanese company, as well as the first and second branch stores, are selling them, and buyers are already extremely crowded.

Tianan Foreign Firm at 218 Sichuan Road proclaims that the Firm is the sole agent for the British "Cow Shed" brand of milk substitute powder with the broadest sales and the most efficient benefits. Since it was transported to China and sold, it has gained a great reputation in less than a year, and sales have increased daily because it is rich in nutrients and preserves the original vitamins using scientific methods, and it is completely manufactured without manual labor. Infants who regularly drink Cow Shed brand milk substitute powder can be permanently free from stomachitis, enteritis, diarrhea, and sleep deprivation.

Zhang Heshun Flour Mill at the intersection of Qiujiang Road and Chenjiazhai Road in Zhabei proclaims that the Mill is an old store with decades of outstanding reputation. All of its products are unparalleled in the flour category, such as glutinous rice flour, japonica rice flour, mung bean flour, fried rice flour, broad bean flour, soybean flour, etc., which are elaborately made by hand and are extremely hygienic. Sugar and food stores in the north and south of the city uniformly purchase and use them.
